Implemented a Win32 process access analyzer in C++ that enumerates processes,
identifies matching PIDs, and tests multiple OpenProcess access rights against live targets,
reporting success/failure per mask.Found 1 matching process(es) for: notepad.exe

Found 1 matching process(es) for: explorer.exe
